Local Correspondence 2

Suzhou 75

A Robbery Case Occurs in the City. In the vinegar warehouse alley inside the Fengmen gate, at the house with number 56 occupied by the Chai family, a robbery happened in July of last year. After this incident, it has been a year, only two or three suspects have been found, but the real stolen goods and robbers have not been caught. To everyone's surprise, yesterday (30th) morning at about 4:00 AM, four robbers suddenly came to the Ge Yuanlong Trauma Clinic, number 5 of the vinegar warehouse alley. They came under the pretense of needing medical attention and then proceeded to rob. The details are as follows: In the Ge Yuanlong Trauma Clinic, there is a mother, Ge Wang Zhenru, (age 69) who also treats people's injuries. They hired a rickshaw puller named Feng A Si, which has been two years. After Feng A Si came to the Ge family, he was considered relatively reliable. Recently, Feng suddenly changed his attitude, because he knew that the owners of the house were only the elderly Ge Wang Zhenru and her young grandsons, Jin Fu, Zhen Shan, daughter-in-law, and female worker Guo Wang Shi. Therefore, on the 29th, he pretended to be sick and asked for leave, and hired Xiao Yang to take his place. After Feng asked for leave, he returned to his home at number 2, Huizhu Lane, Dutaiping Alley, and gathered four people, including Huang Jiuzhang, Kong Zhaoyang, Zhang Rifu, and Dai Xiaomao. They discussed at his home a plan to rob the homeowner. At 4:00 AM yesterday morning, Feng A Si accompanied Huang Jiuzhang and the other three to the Ge family's front door. At this time, Ge Zhenru and her grandson Zhen Shan had already gotten up. Feng A Si entered first to find out that Ge Yuanlong did not live at home the previous night. So he took a copper coin out to wet it. He then ordered Huang Jiuzhang to enter and rob. After the four bandits entered, one bandit pretended to have a leg injury, so Ge Wang Zhenru crawled over to examine and treat it. Unexpectedly, another bandit used cloth to cover Ge Wang Zhenru's eyes and did not allow her to make a sound. One bandit was keeping watch outside, and another bandit took off two inlaid gold rings and one pure gold thread ring from Ge Wang Zhenru's hand, as well as one round pure gold bracelet from her arm. At that time, Ge Wang Zhenru resisted slightly, and the bandit knocked out one of her front teeth, and blood flowed like a waterfall. After the bandits obtained the stolen goods, they fled to the nearby Jiaguan alley. Afterwards, Feng A Si then returned from wetting the coin, and accompanied Ge Wang Zhenru to report to the second branch of the Public Security Bureau in the alley. Then Ge Yuanlong also went to the bureau to report. According to Ge Wang Zhenru, the bandits resembled rickshaw pullers. After receiving the report, the head of the Pan branch telegraphed the detective team to assist in the arrest, and ordered the police in the bureau to search everywhere to track down the robbers. Then, Wang Xing San, a police chief from the flying squad, was investigating the household of a police officer named Ding Jie, and arrested Huang Jiuzhang in the Waque Lane. Xue Yijun, a detective from the detective team, and Huang Ziyun, a police officer from the branch bureau, arrested Kong Zhaoyang at the entrance of the Chayuan Square in Guanqian. Detective Wang Wenyuan and others arrested Zhang Rifu inside the Panmen gate. Zhang patrol officer from the bureau went to the uncle of Zhang Rifu, Zhang Da Laohu stove in the Gaodun lane mouth in Wuque bridge to search for the original stolen gold bracelet and three gold rings. It was taken after the head of the Pan branch briefly reviewed it, that the case was instigated by Feng A Si, and he confessed to the robbery. The head of the Pan branch then ordered the chief of police to detain Feng A Si to be sent to the bureau for investigation and prosecution. Dai Xiaomao escaped.

Lu Yiren Released on Bail. Lu Yiren, a local thug from Haimen, colluded with bandits and refused to accept the judgment of the Dantu District Court. He came to Suzhou in the spring to appeal to the High Court, but it has not yet concluded. He planned to apply for bail the day before yesterday, and the High Prosecutor's Office has approved it, approving a written bail of 5,000 yuan. After receiving the approval, Lu found Hong Shao Pu, the former president of Suzhou Bank, to guarantee his release yesterday (30th).

Wuxi 76

New Details on the Robbery of a Steamboat and Kidnapping Case. A case of lake bandits robbing a steamboat, kidnapping people, shooting and killing a water police guard, and robbing weapons occurred near Wangyewan in Hengjing, Jiangsu Province, at 7:00 AM on the 23rd of this month. The Department of Civil Affairs appointed Gong Guoliang, District Chief of the Third District, as the commander of the Taihu Bandit Suppression, and joined with the Suzhou-Wuxi Water and Land Police Force to encircle and suppress the bandits in the lake. He had already organized a temporary headquarters in Suzhou yesterday. Mao Mujun, District Chief of the Second District, is currently stationed in Dongshan, constantly patrolling the lake surface. He once encountered a bandit ship, but was unable to catch up and was forced to flee to Zhejiang Province. District Chief Gong received a letter from the bandit side yesterday, stating that Wang Wusheng, the captain of the Eighth Team, and the 27 hostages were all safe, but a large sum of money was required (one said 500,000 yuan) before they could be released. In addition, the conditions were also harsh. Wang Wusheng's family has also received a letter from Wang, stating that he is being well-treated in the bandit's den, but he must obtain a large sum of money before he can be free. According to the letter, in addition to actively suppressing the bandits, a team was sent to Shanghai to negotiate with the bandits in order to balance toughness with flexibility. As for the bandit organization, it is actually made up of the Pudong and Chaohu gangs of Hunan. The general headquarters is in Shanghai, and although Zhong Zhaokui is coming forward, there is actually another person behind him, and there is a background.

Mediation Meeting on Labor-Management Disputes in Silk Factories Today. The labor-management disputes in silk factories have not been resolved for a long time. Recently, both parties requested the county government to mediate impartially, and County Magistrate Sun invited representatives from the county party and government, the county chamber of commerce, and the labor and management association to hold a preliminary meeting last Wednesday to exchange views. On Thursday and Friday, he summoned representatives from both the factory and labor sides to the county to inquire about the truth. He has a clear understanding of the content of both parties and the crux of the problem, and he has concrete solutions. In accordance with the regulations on handling labor-management disputes, he has scheduled a meeting at the county government at 2:00 PM on the 31st to convene representatives from both parties and party, industry and commerce to mediate.

Police Chief Commits Suicide Due to Poverty and Illness. Zeng Jixiong, the police chief of the Tenth Sub-Bureau of the Ninth District (North) Public Security Bureau, has been suffering from illness recently, which comes and goes. Although he has been treated, it has not been effective. He also felt that it was difficult for a family of several people to make a living. On the 26th, he invited Wang Ming, an employee of the bureau, to his home and asked him to send a letter to his brother, saying that he had been ill for a long time and was determined to commit suicide. After Wang returned to the bureau, he reported the information to Bureau Chief Wang Weixin, who immediately sent a letter to Zeng's home to inquire about him. The day before yesterday, he sent Police Officer Chen Yunlong to deliver 10 yuan, instructing him to rest and recuperate. Unexpectedly, that afternoon, Zeng suddenly threw himself into the river and committed suicide. By the time he was pulled up, it was already too late to save him. It is heard that his funeral was desolate and that he left behind a widow and orphan in extremely pitiful circumstances.

A Buggery Case Occurs in the Northern Township. In the Sanghe area of ​​Xiyi Northern Township, there is a named Shigen, who is engaged in the bamboo ware industry. Recently, he had same-sex love with a certain A living at Huili, Hanchang Road, outside of the Guangfu gate, because the back part of A has a special state, is different from ordinary people. At about 4:00 PM yesterday, Shigen again practiced buggery at A's home. Unexpectedly, Shigen's wife, Lan Ying, heard about it, and burned with anger. She immediately broke down the door and entered the room to catch the adulterers, and found that the two were sleeping face to face. She immediately grabbed them and twisted them into the police station, asking for legal action.

Drastic Fall in Rice Prices Shortens the Date of Price Stabilization. This year, the price of rice in this county has gradually soared, becoming unstoppable. Gaobai rice has risen to as high as 19.67 yuan per shi, which has seriously affected the livelihood of the poor. It is generally expected that in June and July, during the lean season, the price of rice per stone will break the 20-yuan mark, and no one is not hoarding it to wait for a good price. Unexpectedly, in the recent ten days, more than 200,000 shi of foreign rice were shipped into our county, so the price of rice suddenly plummeted. Yesterday, the market price of white rice was only 16.5 yuan per stone, and the price of dumplings was about 12 yuan per stone. However, no one asked about the rice stored by the unscrupulous merchants. When the price of rice was high, the county chamber of commerce convened a meeting of various industries to raise funds for stabilizing prices. Because the price of rice has fallen, the price stabilization date has been shortened, and the donation money recognized by various industries has been returned by half. Yesterday, special letters were sent to various industries to come and collect the receipts. At present, the price of rice on the market has a tendency to continue to fall, which is a boon for the future of the people's food.

A Knife-Wounded Man's Body Found Hanging in a Deserted Tomb. In a deserted tomb near Qianqiao Town, Nianbaer Tu, Kaiyuan Township in the county, an unnamed man's body was suddenly found hanging the day before yesterday. The Tu Zheng (township head) of the Tu, Miao Yu Gui, came to the city to report to the county government and requested an inquest. After receiving the report, the county government commissioned the coroner Yu Chengshen, accompanied by the examiner Shen Guifang, and the government police, to take a boat to the countryside at 2:00 PM yesterday to conduct a legal inquest. It was found that the deceased was about 20 years old, with a silk rope mark on his throat. The earguards were not crossed in a figure of eight. There were two scissor stab wounds below his genitals (commonly known as egg belly). There was no other reason for the commissioner to believe that he had committed suicide after his male organs were injured during his lifetime. After the inquest, the coroner Yu Guigui was ordered to collect the body, cut the corner, seal it, and send it to the altar for temporary placement, awaiting identification by the corpse family.

Changzhou 77

The Entire Town of Cuiqiao Robbed: On the 29th, at around 7 p.m., a [covered boat] arrived at Cuiqiao Town, Sixth District, Wuyi County, carrying over thirty bandits. Armed with guns, they landed and proceeded to the First Sub-Station of the Tenth Branch Bureau of Public Security in the town. They robbed the station of its firearms, shooting and killing the guard, He Yinsheng. All six Ma Tieli quick-firing rifles in the station were taken. Subsequently, they dispersed throughout the town, robbing various shops and residences, with no one spared. The most significant losses were suffered by approximately seven or eight households. The stolen goods were loaded onto a captured civilian boat down by the river. By the time the nearby Qishuyan and Henglin land and water police and local defense forces arrived, the bandits had long fled. The town is temporarily being garrisoned by a unit of water police.

Continued Arrests in the Bianziqiao Bandit Case: Cheng Zhuozhang, a patrol officer from the Fourth Sub-Station of the First Branch Bureau of Public Security outside Xiaobeimen in Wuyi County, had previously cracked a bandit den in Bianziqiao on the 28th of last month. He arrested Sun Tianbao's family members, Sun Jide and Sun Wangshi, along with a large amount of stolen goods. On the 1st of this month, he further arrested Bian Zhonghe. All were handed over to the County Court for interrogation. On the 29th, at noon, patrol officers from the station arrested a bandit named Cao Hongde in Xiaoyingqian within the city. Cao confessed that the previous robberies were led by Wu Jinquan. He also stated that a White Langlin pistol from one of the cases had already been sold. Upon receiving this information, Officer Cheng, accompanied by Cao Hongde, rushed to Bei Hou Street and apprehended Wu Jinquan and his concubine, Wang Gaoshi. A large amount of stolen goods was found in their residence. They confessed to the robberies without hesitation. Finally, Xie Yangshi, another bandit's concubine, was arrested in Room 6 of the Chen Family Inn under the Dafu Bridge. All the apprehended individuals and evidence were handed over to the court on the 30th for interrogation.

Nantong 78

City Shops Close Again: On the 28th, rioters caused disturbances in Nantong, robbing police of their weapons and releasing prisoners. All the shops in the city closed down. That evening, the military and police temporary garrison recovered the lost weapons and arrested two ringleaders. The county government also dispatched a county police unit to the city to maintain order. On the morning of the 29th, the Nantong-Chongming-Haimen-Taizhou General Chamber of Commerce urged all businesses to reopen. However, at noon, a crowd gathered again in the west of the city, and the garrison immediately dispatched units to stop them. All shops closed down simultaneously. The General Chamber of Commerce convened an emergency meeting to discuss how to handle the situation and appointed representatives to petition the county government.

Accused Police Officer Dies in Prison: Jiang Chuntang, the owner of the Lu Shunhai carriage business in the Xincheng Market in the south of the city, was beaten to death by Liang Qinghai, a police officer from the County Police Department. Liang Qinghai was handed over to the court for interrogation by Captain Jin. Before a verdict could be reached, Liang suddenly died in prison on the 29th. The death was confirmed by the court. The body was prepared for burial.

Bandits Surrender, Awaiting Headquarters Decision: The office established by the Jiangbei Guerrilla Headquarters in Nantong and 19 other counties has completed the first phase of [adjustment] work and is continuing with the second phase of suppression and pacification. For bandits who surrender, except for those who are wanted, all cases are submitted to the General Headquarters for a decision.

Request Submitted to the Provincial Government to Remove the Director of the Construction Bureau: The director of the County Construction Bureau, Yao Pengnian, has been reported by the Party headquarters on numerous charges, and a request has been submitted to the provincial government for his removal.

Jiangyin 79

Collection of Boat Tax Still Under Consideration: Shi Yulin, Sha Ruiying, and others, proposed establishing a Jiangyin County boat tax in Jiangsu Province, modeled after Zhejiang and Anhui, to increase national treasury revenue. They also drafted organizational regulations, with the tax based on the size of the boat, charging 50 cents per zhang (approx. 3.3 meters) in length, with larger boats taxed accordingly. They submitted this proposal to the Department of Finance for approval. The Department of Finance stated that according to the central government's standards for dividing national and local taxes, boat tax was not included in the provincial local tax revenue. Currently, during the deduction and compensation period, the Department of Finance is planning to handle this matter. However, to determine how much revenue the Jiangyin boat tax could generate annually and the status of ships entering and leaving the port, the Department of Finance ordered the Financial Bureau to investigate and report. Director Shen, upon receiving the order yesterday (29th), sent a letter to the Construction Bureau to investigate and report to the Department of Finance for review.

Editor of the "Ping Bao" Arrested and Detained: The County Party Committee Rectification Committee, due to the "Plain Talk" column in the "Ping Bao" newspaper on the 26th and 27th of this month, with articles signed Qin Nan Ala and Amitabha's Nine Sutra Dreams, which were deemed insulting to the Rectification Committee, sent a letter to the Public Security Bureau to summon the editor, Dai Yuelun, to the county. In the afternoon of the 29th, Examiner Yang Cheng interrogated Dai, who claimed the articles were playful and not directed at anyone. Dai also stated that the "Jiangyin Evening News" was not edited by him. As a result, he was ordered to be temporarily detained by the Public Security Bureau, with a fine to be announced today (30th) in the morning.

Jingjiang 80

Conflict Between County Police and Public Security Branch Bureau Over Soil Investigation: On the morning of the 23rd, according to a report from Detective Yao Maotang, a large shipment of opium would be transported from Hankou that night. County Magistrate Wang immediately ordered the police squadron leader, Wang Gongyi, to personally lead twenty plainclothes officers to lie in wait at the ports of the 4th, 5th, 6th, 7th, and 8th weirs. Around 1 a.m., a Jardine Matheson's Whampoa steamer arrived from upstream and unloaded passengers at the 8th weir. Sure enough, many opium dealers were carrying loads on their shoulders and in their hands, disembarking one after another. After inspection by the water police and the Public Security Branch Bureau, the county police carried out a third inspection. The opium dealers immediately said, "We have already made arrangements, there is no need to inspect again." They also asked, "Which unit are you from?" Upon hearing this, the county police were certain they were opium dealers and proceeded to arrest them. Dai Ziping, the water police patrol officer of the 8th weir, Chen Yi, the director of the Public Security Branch Bureau, and the third regiment commander of the 7th district, upon hearing the news, led their units to the scene and ordered the arrest of the "bandits" without asking for any details. The county police officers presented their identification symbols, but Bureau Chief Chen did not bother to check and instead ordered the officers to beat them, resulting in injuries to officer Ma Chenglong. The opium dealers took the opportunity to escape, and a security regiment member even helped carry three loads of goods, while Patrol Officer Dai personally took away one package. Detective He Fengshan of the county police then grabbed a female opium dealer, Li Wangshi, and found 21 packages of opium on her, weighing a total of 42 ounces. The Public Security Bureau took the group to the bureau, where the officers were guarded by police, and their weapons and symbols were confiscated. After a while, Squadron Leader Wang heard the news and rushed from the 7th weir, showing the secret order to Bureau Chief Chen for inspection. Bureau Chief Chen then released the detained officers and blamed them for not informing him beforehand. Squadron Leader Wang argued that the secret order required strict confidentiality and could only be revealed as a last resort. Bureau Chief Chen disagreed, and another conflict arose. A county police officer, dissatisfied, questioned Bureau Chief Chen and engaged in insulting behavior. Later, both sides reported to the county government. Ma Chenglong's waist was found to have injury marks, and a certain officer was accused of insulting his superior. County Magistrate Wang ordered 200 strokes of the military stick to be administered as a warning. Li Wangshi's opium dealing case was sentenced to four months of imprisonment and a fine of 4,800 yuan. Director Chen and Squadron Leader Wang will be prosecuted separately by the judiciary.

Rugao 81

Clash Between Local Militia and Bandits in Caojiabu: Around 3 a.m. the night before (the 25th), approximately five to six hundred bandits were spotted near Caojiabu, Matang, having infiltrated from Nantong. They killed a township head and kidnapped several people. The local militia engaged them, and after a prolonged battle, the police and local militias from Matang [Gang] and other places arrived and surrounded the bandits. By the time the main force arrived to provide reinforcements, the bandits had already fled. They are currently being pursued.

Another Change of Public Security Bureau Chief: Ding Weijun, the director of the Rugao Public Security Bureau, has been dismissed from his position. The Department of Civil Affairs has appointed Wang Qiying as his replacement. Wang arrived in Rugao yesterday (the 27th) and assumed office today.

Zhenjiang 82

Preparing for the Establishment of a Construction Bond Fund Management Committee: The regulations for Jiangsu Province's construction bonds were previously approved by the 102nd committee meeting of the Legislative Yuan. The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance has scheduled a meeting to convene representatives from the auditing agency, the Department of Construction, the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce, the Zhenjiang Chamber of Commerce, the Banking Association, and the Money Exchange Association to organize the Jiangsu Province Construction Bond Fund Management Committee. Preparations are underway, and a meeting will be convened within days to discuss the matter.

Warrant for Xu Yaoting: The Department of Civil Affairs, based on a report from the magistrate of Suqian County, stated that Xu Yaoting was posing as a recruiter within the county. Suspicious letters were found, and a warrant for his arrest was requested. The Department of Civil Affairs has instructed all subordinate agencies to strictly apprehend him.

Two Kidnappers Transferred to Court: The provincial Public Security Bureau's investigation team previously apprehended two bandits, Sun Youcai and Zhu Guanyou, and a ticket watcher, Chen Wangshi, in connection with the kidnapping of Zhang Hebao's family in Danyang. After interrogation by the bureau, they were transferred to the court yesterday for punishment.

Luhe 83

Large Quantity of Opium Seized in Guabu Town: Opium trafficking is rampant in Luhe, and incidents of transporting and robbing opium are frequently seen. A boat suddenly arrived in Guabu Town a few days ago. It was armed, and refused to be questioned by the local militia, leading to armed resistance and causing disturbance throughout the town. The District Office suspected they were bandits and reported to the county government. The boat was found to be fully loaded with opium, and one person named Liu was captured and sent to the county. Liu confessed to transporting six loads of opium. However, the militia only presented 48 and a half catties [approx. 29 kg] to the county. County Magistrate Liu is paying close attention to the case, pursuing the remaining opium, and reporting to the Provincial Department of Civil Affairs for instructions.

Yangzhou 84

Increased Salt Price to Fund Field Police: The Salt Commissioner of Lianghuai previously received a report from the Tongtai General Field, forwarded by the Field Salt Merchants Association, requesting an increase of 1.5 li (0.0015 yuan) per catty in the price of salt to fund the expenses of establishing a Huainan Field Police force. The Salt Commissioner forwarded the request to the Salt Affairs Office and the Ministry of Finance for approval. Instructions have been received to approve the request. The Salt Commissioner has notified all salt banks in Huainan, Waijiang, and Neijiang, as well as salt sellers in Dongtai, to increase the price of salt by 1.5 fen (0.015 yuan) per shi (approx. 50 kg), and to increase the retail price by 1.5 li per catty.

Pinghu 85

Seven Bandits Executed by Firing Squad: The Second Battalion of the Provincial Security Force stationed in Pinghu previously apprehended 17 bandits, including Miao Lansheng, in Xincang and Yaqian. Battalion Commander Zhao sent them to the Provincial Security Office in Hangzhou for legal proceedings. The Security Office interrogated the bandits, and Miao Lansheng, Hu Jinhai, Hu Asi, and four others confessed to robbing Xincang and Yaqian. They were sentenced to death and executed by firing squad at the scene of the crimes. The remaining ten were imprisoned. On the 28th, troops were dispatched from the province to escort them to Pinghu and then to the scene of the crimes for execution.

Huzhou 86

Bandit Who Robbed a Car Executed by Firing Squad: In early July, a gang robbed a Hangzhou-Changxing bus in Lijiaxiang, Changxing, causing losses of nearly a thousand yuan to the passengers. After the incident, detectives from the city's Bandit Suppression Department investigated and apprehended a bandit named Zhang Yao, who was handed over to the department. The military tribunal interrogated him, and the bandit confessed to the robbery. Yesterday morning, he was brought out, his identity was verified, and he was taken to Lijiaxiang to be executed by firing squad.

Large Number of Refugees Arrive in Yigao Town: Around 1 p.m. yesterday, over two hundred refugees, men, women, and children, suddenly arrived in Yigao Town, north of the city. It was reported that the refugees mostly came from Jiangsu. Upon arriving in the town, their actions were improper and threatened to cause disturbance. The town's security forces, fearing that the refugees might act out of line and disrupt local security, were on alert. They telegraphed the city's Public Security Bureau, requesting police to be dispatched to suppress any unrest.

Hangzhou 87

Hangzhou Rice Prices Gradually Falling: In recent days, a large amount of rice has arrived from the Shu River, causing rice prices to fall. High and mid-grade rice has fallen by 1.67 to 2 yuan or more, while low-grade rice has fallen by 4 to 4.56 yuan. However, retail prices have not yet been reduced. The County Party Committee has requested the Rice Price Assessment Committee to suppress and stabilize rice prices. Losses from the Hurricane: From the morning of the 28th, a hurricane and tidal surge swept into the Qiantang River. Dozens of boats were sunk or capsized in the Jianggan to Zhakou area of Hangzhou. Forty to fifty men, women, and children drowned. The loss of bamboo, wood, and other goods is estimated at ten thousand yuan. The Qiantang River ferry service was suspended on both the 28th and 29th.

Hefei 88

Conflict Between Two Local Militia Groups Over Bandit Loot: Bandit leader Wang Lihao led several hundred men, carrying looted goods and kidnapped hostages, passing through Jiangxiadian. They were intercepted by Wang Chunxi, the head of the village defense militia. The bandits abandoned seven oxen and many loads of clothing. Subsequently, Wang Zijin, the head of the neighboring village defense militia, came to claim the goods. A verbal dispute erupted, and gunfire was exchanged. As a result, two militiamen from Wang Chunxi's group, Wang Chunfa and Wang Chunhong, were killed, and one militiaman from Wang Zijin's group, Wang Rufan, was killed, and Xia Bangxun was injured. On the 25th, all parties filed complaints with the county government. Court President Tang Yin has appointed Sheng Wanzhou to conduct an on-site investigation.

Chinese Expeditionary Football Team Heads to Java 89

Departed from Singapore on the 18th

Temporarily Using the Name "Lehua Team" in Singapore

Charity Games After Java Tournament to Aid Unemployed Workers in Malaya

(1) Farewell Banquet Before Departure to Java

(July 18th, Singapore Dispatch) The Chinese Expeditionary Football Team, on its way to Europe and the Americas, stopped in Singapore and played two matches. On the 13th, they won 2-1 against the Malayan Chinese team, and on the 16th, they lost 0-3 to the Singapore Combined Team. This information has already been reported in previous dispatches. Last night (17th) at 8 p.m., the team was invited by Mr. Xu Qingmian, the president of the Singapore Chinese Swimming Club, to a banquet held at the Chinese Swimming Club. Many members of the Chinese Swimming Club were also invited to attend. The party continued until late into the night. All members of the team departed for Java this afternoon (18th) and are expected to arrive on the 20th. They will travel throughout the Dutch territories.

(2) Charity Games in Kuala Lumpur

This time, the Chinese Expeditionary Football Team is temporarily using the name "Lehua Team" in Singapore. The Hua Nan and Hua Football Teams have come south one after another, attracting the attention of people in the southern region. The Chinese Team originally intended to travel together, but due to various reasons, it could not be done. However, players Cao Guicheng and Chen Guangyao of the Chinese Team have already come with the Lehua Team. Thus, it can be said that three of the Chinese players have met with people in the southern region. After they compete separately, they will form a team and rename it the Chinese Expeditionary Football Team to travel to Europe. However, after arriving in the southern region, the Lehua and Hua Nan teams, aware that the prices of rubber and tin in Malaya are declining daily, causing great suffering to the people, and that the number of unemployed people is increasing daily, filling the streets, feel strongly that these unfortunate people urgently need relief. Philanthropists in Kuala Lumpur are actively seeking ways to provide relief, which is also a matter of urgency. The players, aware of this situation, have volunteered to help. They plan to fulfill their commitments in Dutch Java first. After completing their matches there, they will return to Kuala Lumpur and invite teams from various cities in Malaya to form a selected team. They will hold a special match on a selected date, and half of the proceeds from ticket sales, after deducting expenses, will be used to maintain the unemployed workers. Currently, everything is actively underway. It is hoped that when this event is completed, the unemployed workers will be grateful.

Important News

Inspection of Military Education Achievements in Jiangsu and Zhejiang 94

The Training Department Requests the Ministry of Education to Review and Implement Rewards and Penalties for Various Principals

The Training Supervision Department previously sent personnel to inspect military education in high schools and above in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces. This has now been completed. People in society and officials from schools in Jiangsu and Zhejiang are eager to know the results of the inspection and the comparisons made. The reporter has learned that the department's letter to the Ministry of Education provides a detailed account of the inspection of various schools and has separately imposed rewards and penalties. The original text is reproduced below:

Training Supervision Department Advisory (Education No. 79) Regarding the matter of consultation, this department dispatched Lieutenant Colonel Cheng Bingren and Wang Zemin in early April to inspect military education in high schools and above in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces. They returned to the department one after another in June and submitted separate reports on their findings. Now, after a comprehensive review of the performance of each school by this department, with the exception of those with no significant strengths or weaknesses, which will not be discussed,

Those to be rewarded: It has been found that the Jiangsu Provincial Songjiang High School, the Zhejiang Ningbo Private Xiaoshi High School, the Shanghai National Labor University Agricultural College, the Jiangsu Provincial Changzhou High School, the Jiangsu Provincial Yangzhou High School, the Zhejiang Hangzhou Private Physical Education College, and the Zhejiang Provincial Tenth High School have performed well. This demonstrates the enthusiasm and guidance of the principals and the effective training of the instructors and assistant instructors, which is commendable. Chen Jing, principal of Jiangsu Provincial Songjiang High School, and instructor Gan Yanan; Feng Du, principal of Zhejiang Ningbo Private Xiaoshi High School, and instructor Zhang Yuanzhi; Yi Peiji, president of Shanghai National Labor University, Li Lianggong, dean, and instructor Cao Shengwu; Zheng Tonghe, principal of Jiangsu Provincial Shanghai High School, and instructor Cao Wenlin, assistant instructor Chen Bingkai; Jiang Menglin, president of Zhejiang Provincial Senior High School, and instructor Wang Weijian, assistant instructor Wang Yingjun; Jiang Menglin, president of National Zhejiang University, Li Ximou, dean, and instructors Dai Shixun and Lai Xujiu; Zhu Lu, principal of Jiangsu Provincial Changzhou High School, and instructor Ma Guoyong, assistant instructor Bai Hongfei; Zhou Houshu, principal of Jiangsu Provincial Yangzhou High School, and instructor Zhou Chaofan; Kong Yong, president of Hangzhou Private Physical Education College, and instructor Lai Xujiu; Shou Jiajun, principal of Zhejiang Provincial Tenth High School, and instructor Jin Zhenkui should be given a major commendation each in accordance with Articles 2, 4, and 5 of the Regulations on Rewards and Penalties for Military Education in High Schools and Above to encourage them.

Those to be warned: Furthermore, it has been found that Huang Wei, the former military instructor of Donghai High School, was appointed in March of the 18th year of the Republic and left his position in July of the same year. The school concealed this fact and did not report it. In November of the same year, this department ordered the National Military Education Department to directly inquire with the school, but there was no response. It was not until late April of this year that the school reported the matter and requested that Wang Wenying, the school's general affairs officer, concurrently serve as military instructor, intending to perfunctorily fulfill the inspection, resulting in the interruption of military education at the school for as long as ten months. The principal and instructor of the school are hardly blameless. The academic atmosphere of Rugao High School is extremely poor, and discipline is lacking. Shouting and noise can be heard in the classrooms and on the playground. Military education facilities are non-existent, and academic performance is also mediocre, which is negligent. Zhu Lingdou, principal of Donghai High School, and Wu Yingfu, principal of Rugao High School, should be given lenient warnings separately for their failure to effectively implement military education to encourage them to be more diligent. Huang Wei, the former instructor of Donghai High School, should be dismissed for dereliction of duty and permanently barred from appointment. Wu Churui, the instructor of Rugao High School, should be given a major demerit in accordance with Article 11 of the Regulations on Rewards and Penalties to show a minor punishment for his poor teaching and unsatisfactory performance.

Those to be improved: Furthermore, students at Zhejiang Provincial Seventh High School do not understand the academic subjects. The technical subjects, with the exception of the first and second-year students of the Normal Department, are not only unskilled but also lack enthusiasm and appear to be acting as children. The reasons for this are (1) the principal and instructor have different opinions, (2) the number of students is too large, and one instructor cannot handle them all. Principal Fang Hao and instructor Xie Dingyuan of the school should be ordered to pay attention to this matter and make improvements. Furthermore, only one-fifth of the students at Shanghai National Jinan University receive military training. Although the performance is good, it is not widespread enough, which is not in accordance with the regulations. The school should also be ordered to rectify this.

In addition to the rewards and penalties for military instructors, which have been registered and notified for compliance by this department, the rewards and penalties for the principals are hereby requested to be reviewed and implemented by your ministry in accordance with the regulations, and to be notified to all provincial and municipal education agencies and schools for their information. This is in accordance with official etiquette. Furthermore, it is stated that National Central University and Private Jinling University have not yet been inspected due to the summer vacation. This consultation is to the Ministry of Education, He Yingqin, Training Supervisor.

Order of Performance: Attached is a list of the order of performance of the inspected First District (Jiangsu Province): Songjiang High School, Shanghai High School, Changzhou High School, Yangzhou High School, Zhunyin Agricultural School, Xuzhou High School, Taicang High School, Wuxi People's Education Institute, Wuxi Labor and Agriculture College, Jinling High School, Suzhou High School, Zhenjiang High School, Suzhou Agricultural School, Wuxi High School, Huaian High School, Huaiyin High School, Nantong High School, Nanjing High School, Rugao High School, Donghai High School, Wusong Fisheries School (not yet inspected due to the instructor's leave). List of the order of performance of the inspected Second District: National Labor University Agricultural College, Ningbo Private Xiaoshi High School, Zhejiang Provincial Senior High School, National Zhejiang University College of Engineering, Hangzhou Municipal Physical Education College, Zhejiang Provincial Tenth High School, National Tongji University, Hangzhou Private Huilan High School, Zhejiang Provincial Fourth High School, National Jinan University, Ningbo Municipal Vocational School of Engineering, National Zhejiang University College of Arts and Sciences, National Labor University College of Engineering, National Labor University College of Social Sciences, National Labor University High School Department, Ningbo Municipal Vocational School of Commerce, Zhejiang Provincial Law and Politics College, Zhejiang Private Zhijiang University, National Hangzhou Art College, National Jiaotong University, Zhejiang Provincial Medical College, Zhejiang Provincial Seventh High School, National Zhejiang University Agricultural College (not yet inspected due to the instructor's leave), Zhejiang Provincial Senior Sericulture High School (not yet inspected due to all students being away for practice), Shanghai Private Datong University (not yet inspected due to the instructor leaving the school), National Central University (not yet inspected due to the summer vacation), Nanjing Private Jinling University (not yet inspected due to the summer vacation).

Educational Institutions Must Subscribe to Party Newspapers 96

The Propaganda Department of the Central Party Headquarters believes that educational institutions under Party rule urgently need to implement Party doctrine education. In addition to emphasizing Party doctrine teaching materials and Party doctrine teachers, it has recently sent a letter to the Executive Yuan requesting it to instruct educational institutions to subscribe to Party newspapers to promote widespread publicity and assist in the progress of Party-oriented education. The Executive Yuan, upon receiving the letter, has instructed the Ministry of Education to instruct all subordinate educational institutions to subscribe to Party newspapers immediately if they have not already done so.

Nanyang Middle School Science Building Construction Begins 103

This year marks the 35th anniversary of the founding of Nanyang Middle School. The school's alumni association, in conjunction with the board of directors and the faculty association, launched a fundraising campaign and has now collected a significant amount. It has been decided to first construct a science building, which will include a physics laboratory, a chemistry laboratory, a science and chemistry classroom, a balance room, and a mechanical drawing room. It has been contracted to the Xinchangji Construction Company in this city and will begin construction on August 1st at a cost of 24,000 taels of silver, with completion within three months. It is reported that the entire project will be constructed with steel and concrete, with flat-topped steel windows. The architecture aims for simplicity and practicality. The design and supervision will be managed by the Nanyang Construction Company.

Free Talk

Dismissed with a Laugh – Hai Ke 104

A: You borrowed fifty dollars last month. Remember, it's due tomorrow. Can you return it to me?

B: Of course I'll return it to you. I'm a man of my word and never break promises. However, tomorrow I'll also have to ask you to lend me another hundred dollars. The previous debt can be offset, and you only need to give me ten dollars.

Wife: Our child is simple-minded. There's no need to rush him into marriage. We can wait until he's a bit smarter before he gets married.

Husband: If we wait until he's smarter, he might not be willing to get married. Because most people who get married are simpletons.

A: I really don't understand. Every year, many people drown at sea. Why do so many people still go sailing?

B: That's not surprising. Don't you see, every year many people die in bed. Why do people still go to bed every night to sleep?

Wife: I ask you, in front of our friends, please don't mention me anymore.

Husband: Why not?

Wife: Because if you say I'm virtuous, they'll never believe you. But if you say I'm not good, they'll all believe you.

Chatting with Mei Lanfang – Lao Zhuo 105

Everything is difficult at the start. Do not be the first to act. Who will be after? Mei Lanfang spared no effort to cross the ocean to develop art. To create a new era for Chinese opera. Its merits cannot be concealed. Lanfang has returned with honor. The public who opened the farewell party before. Another welcome party was held in Dahua. Its grand occasion is no less than last winter. Lanfang was troubled by the sweltering heat. Stayed in Shanghai for a few days. Wait for the ship to return north. Nothing to do in his spare time. Talking about his experience in the United States. According to Yun. There is a language barrier between them and us. Relying on interpreters to guide them. Therefore, before the opening, the interpreter must first explain the various dramas to be performed in detail. Let the audience understand it in their hearts first. Then open. This move has been very effective. Four plays are rehearsed every day. Only the first and last dramas are complete. Only two episodes are performed in the middle. When I first arrived in the United States, the first play performed every day was The Palace Man Assassinating the Tiger. The second play was performed by other actors in one episode. The third drama only performs a sword dance or a feather dance. The last drama is Fenhe Bay. In this way, after two weeks. Only then did they change to performing the first play, Drunken Concubine. The last drama is Killing the Family. Only one scene of Killing the Family is performed. Slightly add or subtract the old script. Change student to vice. Yidan is the right ear. After each play is over. Be sure to close the curtain once. And the audience in the audience. Then there is no curtain call. Usually there are four or five curtain calls at most. But sometimes when the audience is warmly welcomed. There are as many as ten curtain calls. The palace people's original intention in performing Ci Hu was to assassinate Li Zicheng. Hu mistakenly hit the deputy car. After the assassination. The palace people also regretted it very much. Viewers pay close attention to this expression. It can be seen that people in America are very aware of drama. Observation is deep and subtle. Also, our country's actors. Can be increased or decreased at will. In the United States, acting is like a stereotype. No additions or deletions are allowed. It also shows one aspect of their strict viewing psychology. The play Drunkard. Only describe the drunken state and jealousy of Concubine. To the original lustful excitement after drunkenness in the play. Made all kinds of dirty gestures with Gao and Pei. All are deleted. The knowledgeable people sighed for the improvement. In summary. The fame of his art is not a coincidence. Lanfang also said. This time, Europeans living in the United States. Very much looking forward to going to Europe via the United States. To comfort the thoughts of the people of his country. But only prepared for traveling to the United States in advance. And did not have time to travel to Europe. And on the side of the office staff. Talents who are familiar with the situation of European countries must be sought. And in terms of drama. Also, how to improve and adjust. All can be settled in a short time. It is planned to prepare after arriving in Ping. Only this time when I went to the United States twice, I was treated very warmly. Yunyao Jin Feng is refreshing. Go to Fusang to perform for two or three weeks. Has become a promise. Probably going east after autumn. And a certain stage owner on the sea. Then wait for returning from Fusang. A special performance will be retained for several days.

The Serial Murder Case that Caused a Sensation in Yushan – Xuan Xuan Zhai Zhu 106

Xuxiang, Miaoshan Township, the fifth district northwest of Changshu. The Xu family lives in a clan. Therefore, the local name is Yunyun. There is Xu Bingsong, who is over fifty years old. The family is well-off. Bamboo craftsman by profession. He has always disliked his wife. Often scolding for reasons. Even to the point of driving her out. Hiring to make a living. Xu also ignored it. Half a month ago. Xu's wife came back gracefully. He has forty-eight foreign scorpions. All give to Xu. After five or six days. Xu suddenly quarreled with his wife again. The sound reached outside the house. Clansmen are used to hearing it. I don't mind. The next day. Xu locked the door and went out. I can't see his wife. To catch Xu and return to Qunxun. Say he went somewhere else. Before long. Xu's wife's father also arrived. Ask the neighbors everywhere. Gai Xu has already threated his father-in-law. Said to be hiding. Forcing Xun Jiao. The clansmen saw Xu's caution in guarding the gate after his wife disappeared. I always suspect it. Because he informed the township head. The township head said to the district office. The public office forwarded it to the Fifth District Public Security Bureau. Sent patrolmen to the countryside to investigate the details. Xu Yangyang entertained. His expression was natural. When the patrolman was asking questions outside the room. Xu suddenly entered the bedroom. After a while. Suddenly there was a crashing sound. The patrolmen rushed to see it. Xu was lying in a pool of blood. The hands still held the bamboo knife tightly. He cut his throat and died. Very surprised. Returned to the county to report. The county appointed a judge to go to the countryside for inspection. But in the thatched nest in the room, the loose mud was found to be floating. Remove the nest and remove the mud. Xu's wife's body was clearly there. Carry out to inspect it. There was a hemp rope around his neck. A hole pierced the top of the head. Filled with mud. The two legs were cut off. Marinated with salt. Tied to the back of the corpse. So the case is clear. Xu committed suicide out of fear of sin. Xu has no children. Liem was buried by his brother Sheng.

Since Zhenjiang was returned as the provincial capital. All facilities. There has been a lot of progress. I happened to visit here a few days ago. I will choose its trivia. Send the facts in this talk.

More and more hotels in Zhenjiang. The Jiangbian area is the most famous. Compared to the provincial government's move. Crown Gai travels back and forth. Suddenly it was lively. The hotel industry is also developing in a special way. In terms of the new buildings. The Zhenjiang Hotel is the best. All equipment. Completely Western style. The rest, such as Wanquanlou, etc. Also working hard to refresh. Arrangements Chuchu. Every day, the room. Mostly there is a problem of supply falling short of demand.

The cold food business is booming. The weather in the town is hot. Compared to the sea, it's almost too much. Therefore, the cold food business. Extremely developed. Such as the Meishi Li Western Restaurant, etc. All are elegant in the room. Not much different from the top. Kuai Huo Lin is located in the park. Zhenjiang Park is Yushan. In this hot summer. After logging in. Everyone is strangely thirsty. Kuai Huo Lin is located in the middle of the mountain. So the business is booming. The guests are always full.

Cooling off by the river. The Jiangbian area. Relatively empty. By the evening, residents who were cooling off by the river were following each other. But sometimes the sky is clear. The wind does not expose the dust. Even to the river. It can't relieve the heat. Only a steamship is available for rent. You can board the ship and take a spin. Unfortunately, the price is too high. There are few people who ask about it. There are still a few swimming in the river beach. Walking around with companions. No different from the Bund.

Strange lack of Chinese restaurants The Jiangbian area was originally a British concession. Negotiations to take it back. It hasn't been long. Although the market is booming. But if you want to find a Chinese restaurant where you can sit down. Just impossible. Therefore, I walked around a big circle. Went with an empty stomach. Returned with an empty stomach. To talk to classmates. I was laughed at by Xian.

Square Lotus Root – Xiao Ting 108

The fragrance of lotus is ten miles away. The tender lotus root is fresh. Pick it in a basket. Accompanied by iced melon. It is really a good product to relieve the summer heat. Gaoyou Dajing Township. There is a farmer named Yao. A few days ago. Go to the field to pick lotus roots. Watermelon peel boat. Rippling in the stream. Pick four times. Suddenly got a few pieces of strange lotus root. The lotus root is rectangular. Every

It is divided into three sections. Each section is made in a long way. Yao was surprised. After dividing a few pieces and looking at it. I didn't expect that every lotus root hole. Also become a way. Take a look. There is no difference from the old-fashioned coin eye. After this matter spread. People from all over the countryside came to visit. The lotus root is shaped like a round. It is known to everyone. Ice muscle and jade bones. Simulate tender lotus root as jade arm. This is actually a commotion. Good at description. If the lotus root dug by Yao. Then it is not something that we can do. This matter is known to a certain elementary school nearby. Buy a few pieces to go back. Used for reference.

As a result, a group of fans had to change their plans. One after another, they camped in the baseball field the night before. Carry a blanket to keep out the cold. European Tour Newsletter (65) Liu Hai Li 110

(4) An Overview of the Works of 1929 (Below)

To the left of Ponna are three paintings by Charles Guerin. His color is after Cezanne and seems to be more advanced in color beauty. Although he has the meaning of inheriting Cezanne. He also wants to make realism thorough to the extreme. Recently, he has been using passionate eyes to write portraits of modern women. But can skillfully draw the bottom of the hearts of modern women next to it is a large nude painting by Osi Bania Eespagnat. A still life painting. The portraits of these two writers are competing to hang side by side. Probably because they are both colorists with special personalities. So put their works together. Osi Bania gradually moved from Renoir's painting style to more shaky brushstrokes. Exaggerating the feeling of strangeness. Opposite him are two still life paintings by Pirre Laprade. Thickly stacked with strong colors. It is like the pattern of colored glass. Roughly make a high and low feeling painting style. To its left. It is the Parisian fashionable writer Asilang's Asselin "Human Body". It is painted with a naked woman sitting in the middle. A child next to him. A piece of cloth in front. To its left is Favry's "Bath". This is really the most remarkable point in many paintings. Further on is a painting by Galo Per Krobg. These three people are from three different aspects. Each opened an end for the emerging art of France. They occupy an equal position in the modern Paris art world. Favry strongly emphasizes self-emotion. Asilang inherited Sedan and wanted to capture the permanent natural reality from space. Garo then tried to discover new life in the completely barbaric flavor from the primitive aspect. If fine art is only a faithful copy of natural appearance. Then the retina is completely a kind of camera. The hand is only a kind of machine. The work is just like a photo. Favry uses the object as a medium to realize himself. Asilang uses color. The shape is solid to the end. Structure to make the inner self's publication originally the essence of art is not in the copied object. But in the creative self-internality. Therefore, the purer the art, the more directly it can express this kind of inner spirit.

Let's talk about our tour. Oh. What big paintings. What is painted is the tragic situation of Jesus on the cross. That is a painting using modern methods and taking religion as the subject matter. According to the news from the production areas of Tunxi and Wuyuan, most of the tea-making firms have ended their business, and it is expected that this year's tea number will be about 4/10 less than last year.

Miscellaneous Goods: Inferior Canton Twigs Rise One Taël 130

The Shuikeng Tungzhi twigs, selected by Zhuang Ji, arrived in over a thousand boxes the day before yesterday. Yesterday, the various shops in the north and south markets opened for business separately, and all the longan shops distributed them. However, the cost of these inferior twigs has slightly increased, and because the price is suitable here, the market is lively. Therefore, the opening price and market price have both risen by one taël. Textiles: Eastern Fabrics Slightly Soft, Moonlight Velvet Still Rising 131

Native cloth: The trend remains firm. Yesterday, the Southern gang completed over three hundred pieces. Twelve-pound "Human Clock" fine cloth and nine-pound "Cat's Neck Jubao Basin" coarse cloth were almost completely bought up. The Northern gang, including Niuzhuang, Tianjin, Dalian, and other ports, is also quite active. Fine cloth is purchased daily, so even in the off-season, prices are rising rather than falling. Yesterday, only blue "Double Fish" fine twill slightly fell by two and a half fen due to end-of-month loan settlement. "Yang Crane" spot goods are still in short supply. Coarse twill has slightly moved in this street, all for dyeing purposes, and the price is also slightly firm.

Eastern and Western Fabrics: Yesterday, Eastern goods were slightly soft, mainly because the July shipments previously ordered by fellow traders have been arriving in Shanghai in succession these days. The June shipments require loan settlements upon arrival, so opening prices have generally fallen slightly. Yesterday, "Baoqiu" fine poplin fell by two and a half li, colored stripes fell by five fen, and dark-colored "Ting" fell by two and a half li. Cotton flannel remains sluggish. Local customers are hesitant to step forward due to this situation. Moonlight velvet alone is showing a thriving trend. "Large Chicken Cage" has been sold for one taël, nine fen, and two and a half li; "Medium Handle Fuhua" for one taël, eight fen, and two and a half li; and "Small Chicken Cage" for one taël and eight fen, a rise of two and a half li. The reason is the continued rise in the fixed price and the unusually active participation of customers.

Cai Pei, Acting Director-General of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, Assumed Office Yesterday 135

After arriving in Shanghai, Cai Pei, the acting Director-General of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, repeatedly declined the position to Minister Wang. However, after Wang consoled and encouraged him, Cai agreed to temporarily serve as acting director, maintaining the status quo. Yesterday at around 11:00 AM, Cai arrived at the company to assume office. The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company specially hung the Party and National flags to show their welcome. The General Management Office specially dispatched Secretary-General Xu Xiuzhi and Wang Hao, director of the Hankou branch, to greet Cai at the Director-General's office on the second floor. Cai did not bring anyone with him. After arriving at the company, there were no speeches or other formalities. He only invited the current section chiefs and heads of various departments to the office to inquire about the company's situation. He also ordered the heads of each section and department to inform all employees to continue to work diligently, stating that he was temporarily maintaining the status quo. When the National Government appoints a responsible commissioner, he will hand over the position immediately. Currently, all matters will continue to be handled according to the methods of the previous Director-General Zhao, following precedent to maintain this transitional period. Later, Cai met with guests and reporters. There are no changes for the time being.

It is also reported that before Cai's arrival at the company, he consulted with Finance Minister Song Ziwen on financial matters. As a result, 200,000 yuan was allocated from the charter fee to meet expenses.

The Wind Weakened Yesterday 136

Ocean Liners Sailed as Usual

The continuous strong winds in Shanghai and the typhoon entering the country have been reported in previous issues. It is now known that the typhoon has penetrated into the interior. Therefore, the customs storm warning ball has been lowered, and ocean liners have successively left port. The details are recorded below.

The Typhoon in Shanghai Gradually Weakened: Since the night before last, there have been occasional showers in Shanghai, sometimes heavy, sometimes light, sometimes falling, sometimes stopping. Yesterday, the wind gradually weakened, becoming even smaller in the afternoon and with no strong wind sounds in the evening. However, the showers during the day have not stopped, resembling autumn weather.

The Typhoon Penetrated into the Interior: The day before yesterday, the typhoon turned north-west from Wenzhou and entered Jiangsu province, passing between Zhenjiang and the capital, and crossing the Yangtze River to the north. According to a report from the Yangjingbang Observatory at 4:00 PM yesterday, it was then located between latitude 33 degrees and longitude 118 degrees, approximately in the area near Chuzhou on the Jinpu Railway. It is still difficult to predict whether its trend will change or continue north, as its progress was quite slow at that time, and it is also difficult to determine the strength of its force. However, Shanghai has avoided being directly hit.

Ocean Liners Sailed Yesterday: The liners that were prevented from sailing on Monday and Tuesday due to the wind sailed yesterday as the wind gradually subsided. The Jiahe and Wanxiang, bound for Fuzhou, have already departed. The Guangsheng of Jardine Matheson missed its port of entry and will return directly to Hong Kong and Guangdong today instead of going to Qingdao. The Xin Beijing, Xin Ningjing, and Shao, bound for Ningbo, also resumed sailing yesterday. The Chicago, which was delayed outside Wusong for three days, has also arrived in Shanghai. All the ships delayed en route are expected to arrive in Shanghai today.

Mediation Failed Yesterday in the French Concession Water and Electricity Workers' Strike 138

The French Concession water and electricity workers' strike, since its occurrence, has been going on for four weeks, lasting for a long time, causing inconvenience to traffic in the French Concession. Since the central government sent Wang Xingzhou to handle everything and instructed Central Committee member Li Shizeng to oversee the matter nearby, there seemed to be a possibility of a sudden turn for the better within three days. However, according to yesterday's news, the two sides are insisting on their respective conditions, making it difficult to resolve the issue immediately, and there is a tendency for it to gradually expand. The details are compiled and recorded below.

Attitude of Central Committee Member: Since being entrusted by the central government, Central Committee member Li Shizeng has been engaged in mediation. He previously contacted Chen Junyi, a member of the Standing Committee of the Municipal Training Association, by telephone and met him at his residence to discuss the matter. Li expressed sympathy for the workers' strike as a last resort, but also said that prolonged delays are not a long-term solution. It would be best to turn major issues into minor ones and minor issues into nothing. Therefore, his advocacy is to strive to mediate from the root. Yesterday at noon, he invited Chen Junyi to meet again to continue the discussion, but he was obstructed by other matters and the meeting did not take place.

General Assembly: A general membership meeting was held yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM, with over 600 people in attendance. Xu A'mei was publicly elected chairman. After reporting on the conversation yesterday, Chen Junyi of the Municipal Training Association instructed the union to send representatives to contact Du Yuesheng. The union sent Zhou Dexing, Zhang Liansheng, Hu Chunlin, and Jiang A'shan as representatives. Du's mediation conditions included three items: (1) a wage increase of two yuan and four jiao per month; (2) wages to be paid during the strike period; (3) the company to dismiss 50 workers. All the workers unanimously rejected the conditions on the spot. It was then reported that 100 yuan in relief funds had been received from the Support Association. The following resolutions were then made: (1) The company should be responsible for all medical expenses for injuries sustained in the "721" tragedy; (2) An advertising team should be organized to go to all sectors to effectively publicize the cause; (3) A fundraising team should be organized to solicit donations from all sectors to relieve the livelihood of fellow workers; (4) The case of ticket sellers No. 49 and No. 205 assaulting Shen Fusheng, ticket inspector No. 13, should be submitted to higher authorities and the police station for strict investigation and punishment; (5) In the future, any discovered "running dogs" will be dealt with severely by the union.

Staff Meeting: A staff meeting was held at 10:00 AM, with over 170 people in attendance. Chen Hongyuan was publicly elected chairman. The meeting reported on the progress of union affairs and then discussed proposals. Finally, Xu A'mei of the Machinery Department gave a speech, including the following proposals: (1) To send a letter to the board of directors of the French Water and Electricity Company in Paris, urging the Shanghai representatives to quickly resolve the strike without prejudice; (2) To organize an advertising department, with Zhu Zhaohua, Tang Peishun, Yan Yushu, Sun Dianhou, Xu Hongzhao, Tang Keqing, Zhang Huisong, Sun Zhiyu, Fan Sitao, Lu Yongxing, Liu Jiqing, Shen Shengshan, Dai Mosen, and Rao Shuliang as members. A meeting was reconvened at 2:00 PM to discuss advertising methods.

Traffic Department Meeting: A joint meeting of all ticket sellers, track switchers, and lamp operators of the Traffic Department was held yesterday afternoon at 3:30 PM, with over 400 people in attendance. Shen Keming was publicly elected chairman. The meeting reported on the progress and discussed proposals. Finally, Dai Mosen and operator No. 83 gave speeches. The following resolutions were made: (1) Cases of any workers not obeying union discipline or sabotaging the labor movement should be submitted to the Municipal Party Department for disciplinary action according to law; (2) If workers from any department do not attend the meeting, the department heads should be responsible for handling the matter; (3) The case of driver No. 49 and ticket seller No. 205 acting barbarously and assaulting ticket inspector Shen Fusheng should be handled by having all workers be responsible for constantly searching for the residences of the two and strictly arresting and punishing them.

Traffic Department Demands: The workers of the Traffic Department put forward the following demands yesterday: (1) The union has the right to represent the workers; (2) Eliminate fines for letting passengers on after the bell rings and for not shaking the route sign; (3) Eliminate fines for missed stops, missed tickets, and all false accusations by ticket inspectors; (4) No stops allowed without "grease money"; (5) Daily work limited to eight hours, otherwise wages will be increased accordingly; (6) The company should be responsible for any accidental mishaps during driving; (7) No fines for derailments, track departures, or broken bells while the vehicle is on the road; (8) Eliminate harsh penalties for arriving at stops too early or too late; (9) Wages should be paid during the strike period; (10) Track switchers, lamp operators, ticket sellers, and drivers should be treated equally; (11) Workers with minor offenses should not be questioned in the company office; (12) If a roll call is penalized, half a day's wages must be paid.

Declarations of Assistance from Various Unions: The Shanghai-Ningbo Steamboat Servants' Union issued a declaration yesterday in support of the strike of the French Concession water and electricity workers, stating that the union, based on the friendship of the same class and the feeling of "a rabbit mourning for the death of a fox," is willing to lead all workers to pledge their support and fight together to achieve victory. (1) The Fresh Pork Butcher Ship Workers' Union issued a declaration yesterday in support of the strike of the French Concession water and electricity workers, stating that all members of the union are filled with righteous indignation and should give full sympathy and assistance, work together in the same boat, pledge their support, and strive for national glory.

Important News from the Yangtze River Shipping Industry 139

Changsha Telecommunication Stops Cargo Handling: Yesterday, the Changsha gang formally received a telegram forwarded from Hankou, instructing the Shanghai-based merchants to immediately stop purchasing goods and to temporarily store all purchased goods in Shanghai warehouses and not ship them.

Ning Shao's Engine Damaged and Towed to Shanghai: The Ning Shao Company's Lao Ning Shao ship, heading to Yuezhou this time, was heavily loaded with a deep draft. The river water was very shallow in that area, causing the engine blades at the stern of the ship to be damaged and lost, rendering the ship unable to move. A tugboat has been dispatched from Hankou to tow it to Shanghai for major repairs.

British Ships Lower Prices to Compete for Cargo: The British-owned Butterfield & Swire Company's import and export business along the Yangtze River has not been very successful this year, often operating at only 20-30% capacity in recent months. The company has therefore adopted a method of sacrificing costs and lowering fees to attract customers and compete with Chinese and Japanese ships. All import and export freight rates have been reduced to 88% of the original price, and a rebate is also given, with the intention of gaining an advantage in business. This matter is already being implemented.

Negotiations on Sino-Japanese Telecommunications Issues to Begin 142

Formal Negotiations to Begin in September

The National Government has recently been making great efforts to recover the telecommunications rights of various countries. The Da Dong and Da Bei Telecommunications Bureaus have been jointly negotiated by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Ministry of Communications and are in active progress. Japan also has telecommunications bureaus in various parts of China and has had submarine cables in Shanghai, Nagasaki, and other places for sending wired telegrams for a long time. Minister Wang of the Ministry of Communications has requested Foreign Minister Wang to negotiate a solution for recovery. When Foreign Minister Wang visited Shanghai last time, he met with Japanese Acting Minister K. Shigemitsu on the 28th at the Diplomatic Discussion Meeting on Avenue Joffre and negotiated for about an hour. Japanese Acting Minister Shigemitsu has received instructions from the Japanese Ministry of Communications to accept the negotiations. However, detailed procedures still need to be requested from the Japanese government. Therefore, the two parties are currently discussing various preliminary issues and procedures for formal negotiations, exchanging private opinions in advance to prepare for formal negotiations, in order to ensure smooth progress in the future. Acting Minister Shigemitsu and Foreign Minister Wang have agreed to begin formal negotiations in early September. At that time, Acting Minister Shigemitsu will personally go to Jinling to meet with the two ministers of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Ministry of Communications to discuss this issue. The Japanese government agency in charge of this matter is the Ministry of Communications, and it is possible that the Ministry of Communications will send another expert to China to assist in the process.

Overseas Chinese Industrial Survey Group 143

Departing in Five Routes

Overseas Chinese merchants, recognizing the stagnation of domestic production, which has made it impossible to solve the national economy and people's livelihood, have automatically pooled capital and returned to China to invest, seeking to develop various domestic production industries. The general situation has been reported in previous issues. The group has been divided into five teams and has departed for various locations to conduct survey work. The routes are: the first team to the Northeast; the second team to the Northwest; the third team to the Yangtze River area; the fourth team to Guangdong and Fujian; and the fifth team to Yunnan and Guizhou. The members of the group who have arrived in Shanghai have left Shanghai in succession, leaving only one or two people to preside over everything in Shanghai. When the work of each team is completed, they must return to Shanghai for concentration and then return to Southeast Asia for preparation. It is learned that the group has drafted a declaration regarding the industrial matters to be carried out, which will be announced soon. In addition to the group members being responsible for 20 million yuan in capital, other methods will be used to raise funds. A member of the group said that the number of overseas Chinese is over 20 million, and the average property of each person is at least 200 yuan. If each person contributes five yuan, it will be possible to obtain 100 million. If the domestic compatriots can work together with one mind, after ten or twenty years, the motherland will not be difficult to leap to become the richest country in the world.

Jiangsu Provincial Finance Department Issues a Prohibition Against Grain Counter Clerks Committing Fraud 145

The Shanghai County Finance Bureau yesterday received a proclamation issued by the Jiangsu Provincial Finance Department and immediately posted it for public notice. The proclamation stated: "According to the collection of grain taxes in various counties, this department has learned that there are grain counter clerks privately collecting reduced amounts from taxpayers, without issuing receipts, and promising that they will not be urged to vote every year. Ignorant taxpayers are deceived, seeking convenience, and willingly violating the law without regard. Such collusion between superiors and subordinates is encroaching on public funds. How can this be allowed? This proclamation is hereby issued to all grain counter clerks and taxpayers to be aware. If any of the above fraudulent activities are discovered again, the grain counter clerks, being officials and servants, will be immediately handed over to the judicial authorities for aggravated punishment. Taxpayers will be fined five times the amount they should have paid in previous years, in order to deter and punish, without any leniency. All are to comply. This proclamation is hereby issued."

Fundraising for Disaster Relief in Qufu 147

Qufu County, Shandong Province, is the birthplace of Confucius and the center of Chinese culture. All the ancestral tombs and shrines, as well as the artifacts and ceremonial vessels, are models of the Confucian faith and essential items that must be preserved for eternity. The city walls of Qufu are also very ancient. The city is mostly inhabited by descendants of Confucius. Recently, due to the ravages of war, the temples have been disturbed by artillery fire, the markets have been closed, goods have been damaged, and countless people have been killed by bullets. The Relief Committee previously received urgent appeals from various groups in the county. Chairman Xu of the committee especially published a notice in the newspaper soliciting donations of funds and relief supplies. Yesterday, he also came to Shanghai to personally discuss fundraising methods with Wang Yiting, the resident representative in Shanghai, hoping to raise a large sum within a week and send personnel to distribute it as soon as possible. He deeply hopes that people from all walks of life will consider what is at stake for our country's culture and take responsibility for providing relief, donating generously, to show the people's trend towards the Confucian faith, not just seeing it as saving the general disaster victims of the county.

There is Still No Effective Way to Relieve the Cotton Textile Industry 148

The case of relieving the cotton textile industry's finances and reducing and exempting taxes has been submitted by the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau to the Municipal Government for forwarding to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce for review and discussion. It is now learned that the Municipal Government has received a reply from the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, which states that the financial relief for the cotton textile industry is being investigated and handled by the National Goods Bank. As for the request for tax reduction and exemption, the authority belongs to the Ministry of Finance, and it has been forwarded to the Ministry of Finance for review and handling. According to the Ministry of Finance's reply, the reduction and exemption of taxes is related to the national tax quota, and it is being investigated by the Jiangsu Finance Commissioner for review and reply before further review and handling. After receiving the reply, the Municipal Government immediately instructed the Social Affairs Bureau, stating: "It is hereby ordered that the Ministry of Industry and Commerce's reply is approved. After investigation and review by this department, the three points made by the Social Affairs Bureau to resolve the current difficulties are considered essential and have been handled separately. Regarding financial relief measures, the National Goods Bank has been ordered to review and reply. Regarding the request for tax reduction and exemption, it has been forwarded to the Ministry of Finance for review and instruction. Now, a reply has been received stating: After investigating the original request for tax reduction and exemption for the cotton textile products, the matter is related to the national tax quota, and it is being investigated by the Jiangsu Finance Commissioner for proper consideration and reply before further review and handling. It is appropriate to reply for your reference. In addition, it is requested to inform the Social Affairs Bureau for notification. It is hereby ordered." Upon receiving this case and the Ministry of Industry and Commerce's reply, the bureau was instructed to notify them in the numbers 4736 and 5010. With the previous cause approved, the bureau is hereby instructed to notify them and instruct them to comply. This order is issued.

Citizens' Association to Focus on People's Food 149

The Guowen News Agency reports that the Shanghai Special District Citizens' United Association's preparatory committee, in light of the soaring prices and precarious livelihood of the common people in this city, and especially considering the crucial importance of the rice price issue, has organized a special committee to study the causes and effects, investigate hoarding, and determine the appropriate measures for relieving the people's food shortage. It held a meeting and appointed Yu Yangsheng as its representative to go to Mr. Yu Qiaqing of the Chinese Chamber of Commerce to inquire about the details of his relief rice plan and make all necessary contacts. According to reports, the rice price in Shanghai continues to rise and has not decreased, possibly reaching twenty-four or five yuan. This is of great importance to the people's livelihood. Therefore, the Public Works Department, the Municipal Government, and commercial groups have organized a Rice Market Adjustment Committee, raising funds of one

Page 14

million yuan to purchase Xiang rice for subsidized sale. It is reported that large quantities of Xiang rice are being continuously shipped in. Consequently, the rice speculators, upon learning of this, dare not engage in profiteering, and the price has fallen by three or four yuan. However, rice stores are still secretly raising prices, deceiving buyers, or using inferior rice to pass off as premium rice, engaging in trickery for profit. The committee has become aware of these deceits and hopes that your association will investigate the situation separately. Subsidized Rice Continues to Fall in Price 150

Selling Price of 380 Wen Per Sheng

The city's Subsidized Rice Committee, recognizing the drop in rice market prices, has repeatedly lowered the price of subsidized rice to 400 wen per sheng. It is now reported that the committee held its eighth meeting the other day and decided to further reduce the selling price to 380 wen per sheng, effective August 1st. This equates to only 13 yuan per shi. It has been noted that the market price of foreign rice is 14 yuan 67 jiao, while the retail price in rice stores is around 15 yuan, a difference of about 2 yuan per shi. Ordinary people will undoubtedly benefit from this.
